9-32 Decklists
==============



 Posted in **Event Coverage**
 on February 19, 2017 






![](https://media.magic.wizards.com/styles/auth_small/public/images/person/Walkinshaw-Profile.jpg)
By Ray “blisterguy” Walkinshaw











What, the Top 8 decks weren't enough for you? Well lucky for you, I risked almost certain carpal-tunnel syndrome to bring you the rest of the Top 32, because I love you. Yes, all of you. Even that guy back there.
